2. `x**3` (cubic)
3. `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` (nonlinear coupling)
4. `v` (linear in v)
5. `sin(v)` (sine of v)

The term `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` is very unusual - it involves a fractional power of |v| multiplied by x. And `sin(v)` is a sine function of v (not x).

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce both `sin(v)` and `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`:

Most candidates contain terms like `v*Abs(v)`, `v**3`, `v*x**2`, `v*exp(c*x)`, `x*exp(c*x)`, polynomial terms, etc. None of these can produce `Abs(v)**(1/3)*x` or `sin(v)`.

The term `sin(v)` appears in NO candidate explicitly. Some candidates have `sin(...)` but with x-dependent arguments (candidates 32, 44), not purely `sin(v)`.

Candidate 32: `c6*sin(c7 + c8*x + c9*v)` - this has both x and v in the argument. Setting c8=0 gives `sin(c7 + c9*v)`, which could approximate `sin(v)` if c7=0, c9=1. But we'd still need `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` from the remaining terms, which none provide.

Candidate 44: `c6*exp(c7*sin(c8*x + c9))` - this is sin of x, not v.

The term `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` cannot be produced by any of the candidate terms. The candidates have terms like `v*Abs(v) = |v|*v` (which is `sign(v)*v**2`), `v**3`, `v*x**2`, `v**2*x`, etc. None can produce `|v|**(1/3)`.

Even if we tried to approximate `sin(v) ≈ v - v**3/6 + ...`, this is only valid for small v and wouldn't be an exact mathematical equivalence. And we'd still need `x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`.

No candidate contains both `sin(v)` and `Abs(v)**(1/3)` terms (or any equivalent). Therefore, no candidate can be mathematically equivalent to the GT.

[NO MATCH]

None of the candidate formulas can be made mathematically equivalent to the Ground Truth. The GT contains two critical terms that no candidate can reproduce:

1. **`sin(v)`**: No candidate has a sine function of `v` alone. Some candidates have `sin(...)` but with `x`-dependent arguments.

2. **`x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`**: This fractional power coupling term `|v|^{1/3} \cdot x` cannot be generated by any combination of the candidate terms, which only offer integer powers of `v` (like `v`, `v**2*x`, `v**3`, `v*Abs(v)`, `v*x**2`, etc.).

Since mathematical equivalence requires the expressions to match for **all** values of the variables, and no candidate possesses the structural capability to produce these terms, no match exists.

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and compare each candidate to it.

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
`-0.896123622766678*v - 1.29395390256765*x**3 - 1.29395390256765*x*(0.0943056786339846*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 1.29395390256765*x - 0.448061811383339*sin(v)`

Let me simplify:
- `-0.896123622766678*v` = `-2*beta*v`
- `-1.29395390256765*x**3` = `-omega0^2 * x^3`
- `-1.29395390256765*x*(0.0943056786339846*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1)` = `-omega0^2 * x * (gamma*|v|^(1/3) + 1)` = `-omega0^2*gamma*x*|v|^(1/3) - omega0^2*x`
- `-1.29395390256765*x` = `-omega0^2*x`
- `-0.448061811383339*sin(v)` = `-beta*sin(v)`

So GT = `-2*beta*v - omega0^2*x^3 - omega0^2*gamma*x*|v|^(1/3) - omega0^2*x - omega0^2*x - beta*sin(v)`

GT = `-beta*sin(v) - 2*beta*v - omega0^2*x^3 - omega0^2*gamma*x*|v|^(1/3) - 2*omega0^2*x`

With numerical values:
GT = `-0.448062*sin(v) - 0.896124*v - 1.29395*x^3 - 0.12205*x*|v|^(1/3) - 2.58791*x`

The key basis functions in GT are:
1. `sin(v)` - sinusoidal in v
2. `v` - linear in v
3. `x^3` - cubic in x
4. `x*|v|^(1/3)` - product of x with cube root of |v|
5. `x` - linear in x

The critical non-standard terms are **sin(v)** and **x*|v|^(1/3)**. These are very specific basis functions.

## Candidate Analysis

For a candidate to match GT, it must be able to reproduce:
- `sin(v)`: This is a transcendental function of v
- `x*|v|^(1/3)`: This involves a fractional power of |v|

Let me check each candidate for these critical basis functions:

**sin(v)**: Only candidates 32 and 44 contain sin() functions, but they involve sin of combinations with x, not purely sin(v).

**|v|^(1/3)**: No candidate contains `Abs(v)` raised to a fractional power. Some candidates have `Abs(v)` (which is |v|^1) but none have |v|^(1/3).

Since `sin(v)` cannot be expressed as any polynomial combination of `v`, `v^3`, `v*|v|`, `v^2*x`, etc., and `x*|v|^(1/3)` cannot be expressed using `x*v^2`, `x*v`, `v*|v|`, etc., **no candidate can exactly match the GT**.

Let me double-check candidates 32 and 44 which have sin terms:
- Candidate 32: `sin(c7 + c8*x + c9*v)` - setting c8=0 gives sin(c7+c9*v), which with c7=0, c9=1 gives sin(v). But it still needs x*|v|^(1/3) which isn't available.
- Candidate 44: `exp(c7*sin(c8*x + c9))` - this is exponential of sin, not matching.

No candidate has the `x*|v|^(1/3)` term, so none can match.
